<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Principles</h3><a id="user-content-principles" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Principles" href="#principles"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Negative letter-spacing at display sizes.</strong> Every headline at 17px and up carries a slight tracking tighten (<code>-0.12 → -0.374px</code>). This produces the iconic "Apple tight" headline cadence. Never used at 12px or below.</li>
<li><strong>Body copy at 17px, not 16px.</strong> Apple breaks the SaaS convention and runs paragraph text at 17px. The extra pixel gives the page an unmistakable "reading, not scanning" pace.</li>
<li><strong>Weight 300 is real and rare.</strong> Used deliberately on a handful of large-size reads (<code>{typography.button-large}</code> at 18px/300 and <code>{typography.lead-airy}</code> at 24px/300). It's not an accident — it's a light-atmosphere cue reserved for moments where the content should feel airy.</li>
<li><strong>Weight 600, not 700, for headlines.</strong> Apple's headlines sit at weight 600. Weight 700 is used sparingly for <code>{typography.tagline}</code> (21px) when a touch more assertion is needed.</li>
<li><strong>Line-height is context-specific.</strong> Display sizes use 1.07–1.19 (tight). Body uses 1.47. Utility link stacks in the footer/store use an unusually relaxed 2.41 (<code>{typography.dense-link}</code>). The 2.41 is not a bug — it's how the footer's dense link columns breathe.</li>
<li><strong>Weight 500 is deliberately absent.</strong> The ladder is 300 / 400 / 600 / 700. Mid-weight readings always use 600.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Note on Font Substitutes</h3><a id="user-content-note-on-font-substitutes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Note on Font Substitutes" href="#note-on-font-substitutes"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">SF Pro is Apple's proprietary system font. When building off-system:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use <code>system-ui, -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont</code> as the first stack entry — on macOS/iOS/Safari this resolves to the real SF Pro.</li>
<li>For non-Apple platforms, <strong>Inter</strong> (Google Fonts, variable) is the closest open-source equivalent. Inter at weight 600 with <code>font-feature-settings: "ss03"</code> approximates SF Pro's rounded "a" character.</li>
<li>Nudge <code>letter-spacing</code> down by <code>-0.01em</code> on display sizes to re-create the Apple tight feel; Inter's default tracking runs slightly wider than SF Pro.</li>
<li>For body text, tighten line-height by <code>0.03</code> (from 1.47 → 1.44) when substituting Inter — Inter's taller x-height needs less leading.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Layout</h2><a id="user-content-layout" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Layout" href="#layout"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Spacing System</h3><a id="user-content-spacing-system" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Spacing System" href="#spacing-system"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Base unit:</strong> 8px. Sub-base values (2, 4, 5, 6, 7) are used for tight typographic adjustments; structural layout snaps to 8/12/16/20/24.</li>
<li><strong>Tokens:</strong> <code>{spacing.xxs}</code> 4px · <code>{spacing.xs}</code> 8px · <code>{spacing.sm}</code> 12px · <code>{spacing.md}</code> 17px · <code>{spacing.lg}</code> 24px · <code>{spacing.xl}</code> 32px · <code>{spacing.xxl}</code> 48px · <code>{spacing.section}</code> 80px.</li>
<li><strong>Section vertical padding:</strong> <code>{spacing.section}</code> (80px) inside a product tile; tiles stack edge-to-edge with 0 gap (the color change provides the break).</li>
<li><strong>Card padding:</strong> <code>{spacing.lg}</code> (24px) inside utility grid cards.</li>
<li><strong>Button padding:</strong> 8–11px vertical, 15–22px horizontal.</li>
<li><strong>Universal rhythm constants:</strong> the 17px body line-height multiplier (~25px line) and 21px tagline size show up on every analyzed page.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Grid &amp; Container</h3><a id="user-content-grid--container" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Grid &amp; Container" href="#grid--container"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Max content width:</strong> ~980px on text-heavy sections (environment), ~1440px on product grids (store, accessories), full-bleed for product tiles (homepage).</li>
<li><strong>Column patterns:</strong> 3 to 5 column utility card grid on store/accessories; 2-column side-by-side tiles on homepage occasional sections; single-column centered stack on product tile heroes.</li>
<li><strong>Gutters:</strong> 20–24px between cards in a utility grid.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Whitespace Philosophy</h3><a id="user-content-whitespace-philosophy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Whitespace Philosophy" href="#whitespace-philosophy"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Apple's whitespace is the product's pedestal. Every tile begins with at least 64px of air above its headline and 48–64px below. Product renders are never crowded; the nearest content to a product image is at least 40px away. The footer is the only area that breaks this — there, Apple goes deliberately dense to make the full information architecture visible at a glance.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Elevation &amp; Depth</h2><a id="user-content-elevation--depth" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Elevation &amp; Depth" href="#elevation--depth"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Level</th>
<th>Treatment</th>
<th>Use</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Flat</td>
<td>No shadow, no border</td>
<td>Full-bleed tiles, global nav, footer, body sections</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Soft hairline</td>
<td>1px <code>rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08)</code> border</td>
<td>Utility cards, sub-nav frosted-glass separator</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Backdrop blur</td>
<td><code>backdrop-filter: blur(N)</code> on Parchment 80%</td>
<td>Sub-nav and the iPhone buy floating sticky bar</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Product shadow</td>
<td><code>rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.22) 3px 5px 30px 0</code></td>
<td>Product renders resting on a surface (the only true "shadow" in the system)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Shadow philosophy.</strong> Apple uses <strong>exactly one</strong> drop-shadow, and it is applied to photographic product imagery — never to cards, never to buttons, never to text. Elevation in the UI comes from (a) surface-color change (light tile ↔ dark tile) and (b) backdrop-blur on sticky bars. The single shadow is about giving the product weight, not about UI hierarchy.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Decorative Depth</h3><a id="user-content-decorative-depth" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Decorative Depth" href="#decorative-depth"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Atmospheric imagery</strong> on the environment page (photographic vista) supplies mood; no CSS gradient involved.</li>
<li><strong>Edge-to-edge tile alternation</strong> creates rhythm without borders or shadows — the color change itself is the divider.</li>
<li><strong>Backdrop-filter blur</strong> on <code>{component.sub-nav-frosted}</code> and <code>{component.floating-sticky-bar}</code> creates a "floating over content" effect that's functional, not decorative.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Shapes</h2><a id="user-content-shapes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Shapes" href="#shapes"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Border Radius Scale</h3><a id="user-content-border-radius-scale" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Border Radius Scale" href="#border-radius-scale"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>

<tr>
<th>Token</th>
<th>Value</th>
<th>Use</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>{rounded.none}</code></td>
<td>0px</td>
<td>Full-bleed product tiles (no corner rounding)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>{rounded.xs}</code></td>
<td>5px</td>
<td>Inline links when styled as subtle chips (rare)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>{rounded.sm}</code></td>
<td>8px</td>
<td>Dark utility buttons (Sign In, Bag), inline card imagery</td>
</tr>
<tr>

<td>White Pearl Button capsules</td>
</tr>

<td>Store utility cards, accessories grid cards</td>
</tr>

<td>9999px</td>
<td>Primary blue pill CTAs, sub-nav buy button, configurator option chips, search input — the signature Apple pill</td>
</tr>

<td>9999px / 50%</td>
<td>Circular control chips floating over photography</td>
</tr>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Photography Geometry</h3><a id="user-content-photography-geometry" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Photography Geometry" href="#photography-geometry"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Hero imagery</strong>: full-bleed, 21:9 or taller on the homepage; 16:9 on environment and shop pages. Product renders are photographic-realistic, often shot on a tinted surface that becomes the tile background.</li>
<li><strong>Product renders</strong>: PNG/WebP with transparency; rest on a surface tile and pick up the system shadow.</li>
<li><strong>Accessory grid</strong>: square 1:1 crops at <code>{rounded.lg}</code> (18px) radius, light neutral backgrounds, product centered with 20–40px internal padding.</li>
<li><strong>No rounded imagery in hero tiles</strong> — images are full-bleed rectangular. Rounding (<code>{rounded.sm}</code>, <code>{rounded.lg}</code>) appears only on inline card imagery.</li>
<li>Lazy-loading via responsive <code>srcset</code> and <code>sizes</code> across all breakpoints; CDN-optimized WebP.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Components</h2><a id="user-content-components" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Components" href="#components"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Top Navigation</h3><a id="user-content-top-navigation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Top Navigation" href="#top-navigation"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>global-nav</code></strong> — Persistent, ultra-thin black nav bar pinned to the top of every page. Background <code>{colors.surface-black}</code>, height 44px, text <code>{colors.on-dark}</code> in <code>{typography.nav-link}</code> (12px / 400 / -0.12px tracking). Links are quiet, spaced ~20px apart, running edge-to-edge across the top. Right-aligned cluster: Search, Bag icons — always visible. On mobile, collapses to hamburger at ~834px and the Apple logo centers.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>sub-nav-frosted</code></strong> — Surface-specific nav that sticks below the global nav. Background <code>{colors.canvas-parchment}</code> at 80% opacity with backdrop-filter blur, creating a frosted-glass effect. Height 52px. Content on left: product category name ("iPhone", "Store", "Accessories") in <code>{typography.tagline}</code> (21px / 600). Content right: inline nav links in <code>{typography.button-utility}</code> (14px), ending in a persistent <code>{component.button-primary}</code> ("Buy") or a utility link.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Buttons</h3><a id="user-content-buttons" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Buttons" href="#buttons"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>button-primary</code></strong> — The signature Apple action. Background <code>{colors.primary}</code> (Action Blue #0066cc), text <code>{colors.on-primary}</code> in <code>{typography.body}</code> (SF Pro Text 17px / 400), rounded <code>{rounded.pill}</code> (full pill — capsule-shaped), padding 11px × 22px. The full-pill radius IS the brand action signal.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Active state: <code>{component.button-primary-active}</code> — <code>transform: scale(0.95)</code> (the system-wide micro-interaction).</li>
<li>Focus state: <code>{component.button-primary-focus}</code> — 2px solid <code>{colors.primary-focus}</code> outline.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>button-secondary-pill</code></strong> — Used as the second CTA when two blue pills appear together ("Learn more" / "Buy"). Background transparent, text <code>{colors.primary}</code>, 1px solid <code>{colors.primary}</code> border, rounded <code>{rounded.pill}</code>, padding 11px × 22px. Reads as a "ghost pill."</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>button-dark-utility</code></strong> — Global nav actions (Sign In, Bag, language selector). Background <code>{colors.ink}</code> (#1d1d1f), text <code>{colors.on-dark}</code> in <code>{typography.button-utility}</code> (14px / 400 / -0.224px tracking), rounded <code>{rounded.sm}</code> (8px), padding 8px × 15px. Active state shrinks via <code>transform: scale(0.95)</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>button-pearl-capsule</code></strong> — Product-card secondary button. Background <code>{colors.surface-pearl}</code> (#fafafc), text <code>{colors.ink-muted-80}</code> in <code>{typography.caption}</code> (14px), 3px solid <code>{colors.divider-soft}</code> border (functions as a soft ring rather than a visible line), rounded <code>{rounded.md}</code> (11px), padding 8px × 14px.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>button-store-hero</code></strong> — A larger primary CTA used on store hero surfaces. Same Action Blue + Paper White as <code>{component.button-primary}</code>, but with <code>{typography.button-large}</code> (18px / 300 — note the rare weight 300) and slightly more padding (14px × 28px). Used sparingly on the store landing.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>button-icon-circular</code></strong> — Floats over photography. 44 × 44px, background <code>{colors.surface-chip-translucent}</code> at ~64% alpha, icon in <code>{colors.ink}</code>, rounded <code>{rounded.full}</code>. Used for carousel controls, close buttons, and in-image controls (product image thumbnails on the iPhone buy page).</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>text-link</code></strong> — Inline body links in <code>{colors.primary}</code> (Action Blue). Underlined or non-underlined per context.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>text-link-on-dark</code></strong> — Inline body links on dark tiles in <code>{colors.primary-on-dark}</code> (Sky Link Blue #2997ff) — Action Blue would disappear against <code>{colors.surface-tile-1}</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Cards &amp; Containers</h3><a id="user-content-cards--containers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Cards &amp; Containers" href="#cards--containers"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>product-tile-light</code></strong> — Full-bleed light tile. Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code> (white), text <code>{colors.ink}</code>, rounded <code>{rounded.none}</code> (0 — tiles touch edges), vertical padding <code>{spacing.section}</code> (80px). Centered stack: product name in <code>{typography.display-lg}</code> (40px / 600) → one-line tagline in <code>{typography.lead}</code> (28px / 400) → two <code>{component.button-primary}</code> CTAs ("Learn more" / "Buy") → product render resting on the surface with the system shadow.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>product-tile-parchment</code></strong> — Same as <code>{component.product-tile-light}</code> but on <code>{colors.canvas-parchment}</code> (#f5f5f7). Used to break two consecutive white tiles.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>product-tile-dark</code></strong> — Full-bleed dark tile. Background <code>{colors.surface-tile-1}</code> (#272729), text <code>{colors.on-dark}</code>, rounded <code>{rounded.none}</code>, vertical padding <code>{spacing.section}</code> (80px). Same content stack as the light tile but with <code>{component.text-link-on-dark}</code> for inline copy and <code>{component.button-primary}</code> (Action Blue still works on the dark surface). Used on the homepage product grid as the alternating dark band.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>product-tile-dark-2</code></strong> — Variant on <code>{colors.surface-tile-2}</code> (#2a2a2c). Used where a dark tile sits directly above or below <code>{component.product-tile-dark}</code> to create the faintest separation through micro-step lightness change.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>product-tile-dark-3</code></strong> — Variant on <code>{colors.surface-tile-3}</code> (#252527). Used at the bottom of the stack and in embedded video/player frames.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>store-utility-card</code></strong> — Used in store grid and accessories grid. Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code> (white), 1px solid <code>{colors.hairline}</code> border, rounded <code>{rounded.lg}</code> (18px), padding <code>{spacing.lg}</code> (24px). Top: product image (1:1 crop with <code>{rounded.sm}</code> (8px) inner image radius). Below: product name in <code>{typography.body-strong}</code> (17px / 600), price in <code>{typography.body}</code> (17px / 400), and a <code>{component.text-link}</code> ("Buy" or "Learn more"). No shadow by default; product render itself carries the system product-shadow.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>configurator-option-chip</code></strong> — Pill-shaped tappable cell used in the iPhone 17 Pro buy page. Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code> in <code>{typography.caption}</code>, rounded <code>{rounded.pill}</code>, padding 12px × 16px. Contains a small product thumbnail + label + price delta. Arranged in a grid of 4–5 options per row.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>configurator-option-chip-selected</code></strong> — Selected state. Border upgrades to 2px solid <code>{colors.primary-focus}</code>. Same shape, same content.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>environment-quote-card</code></strong> — A photographic-canvas hero specific to the environment page. Dark photographic backdrop (mountain vista at dawn) with <code>{colors.surface-tile-1}</code> as the fallback color, centered white-text headline in <code>{typography.display-lg}</code> (40px), small green "Apple 2030" pictographic logo above the headline, single <code>{component.button-primary}</code> below. Padding <code>{spacing.section}</code> (80px).</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>floating-sticky-bar</code></strong> — Floats at the bottom of the viewport on the iPhone 17 Pro buy page during scroll. Background <code>{colors.canvas-parchment}</code> at 80% opacity with <code>backdrop-filter: blur(N)</code>, height 64px, padding 12px × 32px. Left: running price total in <code>{typography.body}</code>. Right: <code>{component.button-primary}</code> ("Add to Bag").</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Inputs &amp; Forms</h3><a id="user-content-inputs--forms" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Inputs &amp; Forms" href="#inputs--forms"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>search-input</code></strong> — The accessories search input. Background <code>{colors.canvas}</code>, text <code>{colors.ink}</code> in <code>{typography.body}</code> (17px), 1px solid <code>rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.08)</code> border, rounded <code>{rounded.pill}</code> (full pill — search is also pill-shaped, matching the CTA grammar), padding 12px × 20px, height 44px. Leading icon: search glyph at 14px, muted tint.</p>
<p dir="auto">Error and validation states were not surfaced in the analyzed pages.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Footer</h3><a id="user-content-footer" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Footer" href="#footer"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong><code>footer</code></strong> — Background <code>{colors.canvas-parchment}</code> (#f5f5f7), text <code>{colors.ink-muted-80}</code>. Link columns in <code>{typography.dense-link}</code> (17px / 400 / 2.41 line-height — the relaxed leading is what makes the dense columns scannable). Column headings in <code>{typography.caption-strong}</code> (14px / 600). Legal row at the very bottom in <code>{typography.fine-print}</code> (12px / 400) with <code>{colors.ink-muted-48}</code> text. Vertical padding 64px.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Do's and Don'ts</h2><a id="user-content-dos-and-donts" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Do's and Don'ts" href="#dos-and-donts"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Do</h3><a id="user-content-do" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Do" href="#do"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use <code>{colors.primary}</code> (Action Blue #0066cc) for every interactive element — links, pill CTAs, focus signals — and nothing else. The single accent is non-negotiable.</li>
<li>Set headlines in <code>{typography.hero-display}</code> or <code>{typography.display-lg}</code> with negative letter-spacing (<code>-0.28 → -0.374px</code>) to get the signature "Apple tight" cadence.</li>
<li>Run body copy at <code>{typography.body}</code> (17px / 400 / 1.47 / -0.374px) — not 16px. The extra pixel defines the brand's reading pace.</li>
<li>Alternate <code>{component.product-tile-light}</code> (or parchment) and <code>{component.product-tile-dark}</code> for full-bleed section rhythm. The color change IS the divider.</li>
<li>Reserve <code>{rounded.pill}</code> for the primary blue CTA and any other element that should read as an "action" (configurator chips, search input, sticky bar CTA).</li>
<li>Apply the single product-shadow (<code>rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.22) 3px 5px 30px</code>) only to product renders resting on a surface — never on cards, buttons, or text.</li>
<li>Use <code>transform: scale(0.95)</code> as the active/press state on every button — it's the system-wide micro-interaction.</li>
<li>Keep the global nav <code>{colors.surface-black}</code> (true black) — it's the only place pure black appears on most pages.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Don't</h3><a id="user-content-dont" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Don't" href="#dont"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Don't introduce a second accent color; every "click me" signal is <code>{colors.primary}</code> (Action Blue).</li>
<li>Don't add shadows to cards, buttons, or text — shadow is reserved for product imagery.</li>
<li>Don't use gradients as decorative backgrounds; atmosphere comes from photography.</li>
<li>Don't set body copy at weight 500 — Apple's ladder is 300 / 400 / 600 / 700, with 500 deliberately absent. Body is always 400; strong inline is 600; display is 600.</li>
<li>Don't round full-bleed tiles — tiles are rectangular and edge-to-edge; the color change is the divider.</li>
<li>Don't tighten line-height below 1.47 for body copy — the editorial leading is part of the brand.</li>
<li>Don't mix radii grammars — use <code>{rounded.sm}</code> for compact utility, <code>{rounded.lg}</code> for utility cards, <code>{rounded.pill}</code> for pills, and nothing in between (except the rare <code>{rounded.md}</code> Pearl Button).</li>
<li>Don't use <code>{colors.primary-on-dark}</code> (Sky Link Blue) on light surfaces — it's the dark-tile-only variant. Action Blue is for light surfaces.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Responsive Behavior</h2><a id="user-content-responsive-behavior" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Responsive Behavior" href="#responsive-behavior"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Breakpoints</h3><a id="user-content-breakpoints" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Breakpoints" href="#breakpoints"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<p dir="auto">The structural breakpoints that matter for agents: 1440px (content lock), 1068px (small-desktop), 833px (tablet landscape switch), 734px (tablet portrait), 640px (phone), 480px (small phone).</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Touch Targets</h3><a id="user-content-touch-targets" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Touch Targets" href="#touch-targets"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Minimum 44 × 44px. <code>{component.button-primary}</code> lands at ~44 × 100px (with the full-pill radius making the visible hit area more generous than the label suggests).</li>
<li><code>{component.button-icon-circular}</code> is exactly 44 × 44px.</li>
<li>Global nav utility links are smaller (~32 × 80px) — they deliberately sit at a tighter target because they're precision desktop actions, and the mobile hamburger replaces them at ≤ 833px.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Collapsing Strategy</h3><a id="user-content-collapsing-strategy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Collapsing Strategy" href="#collapsing-strategy"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Global nav</strong>: full horizontal link row on desktop → collapses to Apple logo + hamburger + bag icon at 834px and below.</li>
<li><strong>Sub-nav</strong>: category name + inline links + primary CTA → category name + primary CTA only at mobile; inline links move into a hamburger tray.</li>
<li><strong>Product tiles</strong>: stack from 2-column to 1-column at 834px; vertical padding tightens from 80px → 48px at small-phone.</li>
<li><strong>Utility grids</strong> (store, accessories): 5-col → 4-col (1440px) → 3-col (1068px) → 2-col (834px) → 1-col (640px).</li>
<li><strong>Hero typography</strong>: <code>{typography.hero-display}</code> (56px) → <code>{typography.display-lg}</code> (40px) at 1068px → 34px at 640px → 28px at 419px.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Image Behavior</h3><a id="user-content-image-behavior" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Image Behavior" href="#image-behavior"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>All product imagery uses responsive <code>srcset</code> with breakpoint-matched crops.</li>
<li>Hero photography may switch art direction at mobile (e.g., the environment page's vista crops to a taller aspect ratio on mobile, framing the subject differently).</li>
<li>Product renders maintain their 1:1 or 4:3 aspect ratios across breakpoints; only scale changes.</li>
<li>Lazy-loading is default; the above-fold hero loads eagerly.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Iteration Guide</h2><a id="user-content-iteration-guide" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Iteration Guide" href="#iteration-guide"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Focus on ONE component at a time. Reference its YAML key directly (<code>{component.product-tile-dark}</code>, <code>{component.search-input}</code>).</li>
<li>Variants of an existing component (<code>-active</code>, <code>-focus</code>, <code>-2</code>, <code>-3</code>) live as separate entries in <code>components:</code>.</li>
<li>Use <code>{token.refs}</code> everywhere — never inline hex.</li>
<li>Never document hover. Default and Active/Pressed states only.</li>
<li>Display headlines stay SF Pro Display 600 with negative letter-spacing. Body stays SF Pro Text 400 at 17px. The boundary is unbreakable.</li>
<li>The single drop-shadow (<code>rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.22) 3px 5px 30px</code>) is reserved for product photography only.</li>
<li>When in doubt about emphasis: alternate surface (light → dark tile) before adding chrome.</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Known Gaps</h2><a id="user-content-known-gaps" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Known Gaps" href="#known-gaps"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Form validation and error states were not surfaced on the analyzed pages; only the neutral search input is documented.</li>
<li>The homepage's embedded video/player frame uses <code>{colors.surface-black}</code>; interior player controls are not documented (they're a platform widget, not a web-design token).</li>
<li>Some component imagery is dynamic (rotating product hero) and its specific copy varies per surface — component specs name the structure, not the rotating content.</li>
<li>Dark-mode counterparts for store and accessories utility cards were not surfaced on the analyzed pages; the system documented is the daytime/light-dominant variant Apple ships by default.</li>
<li>Atmospheric photography (environment page mountain vista) is a content asset, not a design token; the documented <code>{component.environment-quote-card}</code> describes the structural surface only.</li>
<li>The exact backdrop-filter blur radius on <code>{component.sub-nav-frosted}</code> and <code>{component.floating-sticky-bar}</code> is platform-dependent; production CSS uses <code>saturate(180%) blur(20px)</code> as a typical baseline but the value isn't formalized as a token.</li>
</ul>
</article></div><div class="d-none"></div></section></div></div></div> </div> <!-- --> </div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ScrollMarksContainer-module__scrollMarksContainer__Eu7uU" id="find-result-marks-container"></div><div class="d-none"></div><div class="d-none"></div></div> <!-- --> <!-- --> </div>
</react-app>




  </div>

</turbo-frame>

    </main>
  </div>

  </div>
